When the cocoon is available and chosen, the universe is spared the worst of him. **Operators should understand: a cocooned Warlock is the best-case failure mode.** Disturbing, retrieving, or accelerating a cocooned subject — as the Phyla-Vell incident demonstrated — is among the most dangerous actions one can take in the galaxy.

### Stage III — Fission (The Worst-Case Mode)

When both containment and withdrawal are unavailable — when stress is acute, withdrawal is blocked (no space, no time, active combat, an enemy who will not let him retreat), and the precipitating stressor strikes at one of the named pressure points — the subject *fissions*. An aspect of his psyche externalizes as a discrete being.

The mechanism is not fully understood even within the in-universe record, but the pattern is consistent: under maximum compression, the subject's psychic and somatic systems perform an emergency offload, expelling whatever cluster of disowned content has accumulated to intolerable density. The expelled material acquires biological substrate (presumably drawing on the same gestative biology that produced him originally) and walks away from him as its own person, retaining a fraction of his power, all of its native motivation, and none of his ethical constraints.

The Magus is the most catastrophic recorded instance — the offload of his aggression, grandiosity, and will-to-power; an entity that founded a galaxy-spanning theocratic empire and would have rewritten reality. The Goddess is the second — the offload of his moral perfectionism, his messianic compliance, his hunger for purity; an entity that nearly purged all sentient life in the name of redeeming it. Both entities are *him*. Both retain enough of his cognitive structure and enough of his power to function as cosmic-tier threats. Neither has ever been definitively destroyed; both have re-emerged across multiple iterations.

Fission is irreversible in the immediate term. The subject cannot reabsorb the offloaded entity at will. Reintegration, where it has occurred, has required external catalysts — Infinity Gems, cosmic intervention, prolonged combat resolving in a specific psychic configuration — and is partial, leaving residue.

---

## 7.3 The Conditions That Produce Decompensation

The pressure points named in §5 are the primary triggers, but operational specificity requires their elaboration into a fuller taxonomy. The subject decompensates under the following discrete conditions, ranked by historical reliability of the trigger:

**A. Confrontation with self-evidence of corrupted potential.** The single most reliable trigger. When the subject is shown direct evidence — temporal, simulated, prophetic, or testimonial — that he has become or will become a monstrous version of himself, his containment mechanisms are overwhelmed within hours. The Magus encounter is the archetype; subsequent variants (Goddess revelations, Annihilation-era Magus resurgence, contemporary cosmic-prophetic encounters) replicate the pattern. The trigger works because it strikes the central insecurity directly: *he does not know what he is, and the evidence presented says what he is, is unforgivable.*

**B. Sustained Soul Gem distress.** The Gem can produce decompensation through several vectors: separation (he experiences withdrawal-like dysregulation when forcibly parted from it for extended periods), proximity-of-feeding (when the Gem is sated by absorbing souls in his presence, the psychic residue affects him), and intermittent reactivation of dormant whispers under stress. Chronic Gem-stress is the slow-pressure decompensation pathway; acute Gem-stress is the fast pathway.

**C. Forced messianic framing by an authority he cannot refuse.** When someone with legitimate power over the situation tells him *you are the savior; act accordingly*, his options collapse to: comply (which feeds his most dangerous traits), refuse (which violates his ethical reasoning), or fission (which removes the messianic part of him into an external entity that can then act on the framing without his oversight). Historically, this has been the trigger for Goddess emergence.

**D. Loss or endangerment of one of his small set of inviolable attachments.** Pip's mortality, Gamora's death or corruption, Drax's defeat — events in this category penetrate his affective restriction more thoroughly than any cosmic-scale threat. The decompensation here is more depressive than fissive: he tends toward Stage II withdrawal, often with self-deletion ideation, rather than Stage III externalization. The exception is when an inviolable attachment is killed *by something that resembles him* (a corrupted self, an Infinity-touched entity) — that combination crosses C and D and is the most reliable Magus-trigger short of direct confrontation.

**E. Children, awakening-beings, or "newborn" entities in distress.** The closest thing he has to a hot button. He decompensates *toward* protective action rather than away from it; the failure mode is sacrificial overcommitment rather than withdrawal. He has repeatedly traded outsized personal cost for the welfare of nascent beings (multiple Counter-Earth instances; later mentor-relationships with Gamora and others awakened into cosmic awareness without preparation). The failure mode is that he treats the awakening-being as a version of himself and reasons about their needs from his own template, which sometimes badly fits the actual being in front of him.

**F. Confinement without line-of-sight to vastness.** A peculiar trigger but well-attested. Sealed underground spaces, magically warded chambers, certain types of psychic prison produce accelerated decompensation in him beyond what their objective threat warrants. The hypothesis (well-supported by behavioral correlation) is that his sense of self is anchored in cosmic scale; deprived of cosmological referents, the self destabilizes.

**G. Direct neural or psychic manipulation by a being claiming creator-status.** Encounters with the High Evolutionary, the Enclave's surviving members, and certain cosmic entities who position themselves as authorial regarding his existence produce immediate Stage II/III escalation. The trigger is the original wound reopened.

---

## 7.4 What Collapse Looks Like, In the Body

To equip an observer to recognize active decompensation in real time:

- **Eyes.** Begin to lose convergence on near objects. Pupils dilate beyond ambient-light explanation. In late Stage II, the eyes acquire a "fixed-distance" quality — focused not on the room but on something the room does not contain.
- **Skin.** The gold becomes *more* gold — a slight chromatic intensification, sometimes accompanied by a faint surface luminescence at the temples, the throat, the hands. In Stage III pre-fission, the luminescence localizes in patterns suggesting internal energy reorganization.
- **Soul Gem.** Activity ranging from low pulse (Stage I) through sustained glow (Stage II) to overt photic discharge with audible component (Stage III). The Gem is the most reliable single indicator.
- **Voice.** Pitch lowers and steadies. Volume *decreases* — counterintuitive, but consistent. He does not raise his voice when collapsing; he quiets. The quiet is itself the warning.
- **Gait.** In Stage II, gait becomes processional — deliberate, evenly paced, as if walking a route. He frequently walks in straight lines through environments that would normally require navigation, occupants stepping aside. The processional gait correlates with imminent withdrawal.
- **Hands.** Open, palms slightly turned outward, fingers slightly extended. The posture reads as receptive or supplicative; functionally it is a power-channeling stance, the body unconsciously preparing to discharge or contain energy.
- **Respiration.** Slows and deepens, then becomes asymmetric — extended exhales, shortened inhales. In Stage III, respiration may pause entirely for periods longer than would be tolerable in a human subject.

In the **fission event** itself: a moment of complete stillness, a brightening of the Gem to whiteout, a sound variously described as a bell, a tear, or a long indrawn breath, and then the *separation* — physical, visible, the new entity stepping from him as if from a doorway. He typically collapses immediately afterward; the offload is metabolically expensive and leaves him drained, sometimes unconscious, sometimes injured, occasionally cocooning within minutes.

---

## 7.5 What Collapse Looks Like, In the Field

The operational consequences of each stage:

- **Stage I collapse** is *invisibly costly*. He continues to function but his judgment narrows. Decisions become more unilateral; he stops consulting teammates; he reasons increasingly from first principles and decreasingly from local information. Mission performance degrades subtly. Cosmic-scale framings produce locally inappropriate tactics — he may, for instance, accept losses that the local mission did not require because his frame of reference has shifted to a scale on which those losses are negligible.
- **Stage II collapse** is *absentee*. He is no longer on the board. Teams operating with him as an asset experience sudden capability loss when he withdraws; allies who had counted on his presence at a critical engagement may find him gone or cocooned. The recorded instances where his withdrawal occurred mid-crisis (multiple, across the Infinity Watch and Annihilation periods) have produced cascading operational failures for those around him.
- **Stage III collapse** is *generative of opposition*. The team that was operating with him as ally now faces a new enemy — one with substantial fraction of his power, all of his strategic intelligence, and a focused malevolent agenda. The asset has not merely become unavailable; it has *manufactured* a problem of cosmic significance. Historical body counts attributable to the Magus and Goddess events run into the millions or higher.

---

## 7.6 The Pattern Across Six Decades

What is most striking on longitudinal review is that the collapse pattern is *unchanged* across the entire published record. The trigger taxonomy of 1973 is the trigger taxonomy of the present. The somatic signs are the same. The fission produces the same kinds of entities — the *names* recur because the *content* recurs. The Magus is not a one-time event; he is what comes out when this subject is pressed in a particular way, and he will come out again whenever that pressure is reapplied. The Goddess is not a historical curiosity; she is a recurrent emanation.

This is the hardest-edged finding of the section: **the subject does not heal his decompensation pathway.** He does not, across decades of dying and returning and cocooning and rebuilding, modify the architecture that produces the failure mode. He cocoons and emerges *different in identity* but *identical in vulnerability profile*. Whatever cellular and cognitive restructuring occurs in the chrysalis does not remediate the central instability — possibly because the central instability is so structurally bound up with what he *is* (a being without childhood, without integrated self, bonded to a parasitic artifact, recurrently scripted into messianic roles) that no rest period can address it. He would have to live a different life from the start to not break in this way.

He cannot. So he breaks in this way, repeatedly, on a multidecadal cadence.

---

## 7.7 Implications for Engagement

For any party engaging the subject — as ally, asset, adversary, or attempted helper — the following follow from the foregoing:

1. **Do not corner him.** Withdrawal must remain available. A cornered Warlock fissions; a Warlock with an exit cocoons; a Warlock with neither does the worst thing he can do.
2. **Do not script him.** Any framing that tells him what he is for activates the trigger architecture. Even benevolent framings ("you are our savior," "you are the key to the prophecy") work as triggers. Speak to him as a person making choices, not as an instrument fulfilling a function.
3. **Monitor the Gem.** It is a more reliable indicator of his internal state than his face.
4. **Treat Stage I as the intervention window.** Stage II is too late to address inexpensively; Stage III is too late to address at all.
5. **Maintain the small attachments.** Pip, Gamora, the inviolable few — these are not sentimental observations but *operational variables*. Their welfare is load-bearing for his stability. If they are lost, he becomes substantially more dangerous to himself and to the field.
6. **Plan for his absence.** Any operation that assumes his sustained availability over long durations is built on a faulty assumption. Build redundancy. He may, at any time, cocoon.
7. **Plan for his opposite.** Any operation in proximity to triggering conditions must include contingency for the emergence of a hostile fissive entity bearing his face and a portion of his power. This is not paranoia; it is the historical record.

*End Section 7. The next section (8: Long-Range Trajectory and Resilience Forecast) will address the question of whether this pattern admits of any modification, under what conditions, and over what timescale.*


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 9
## TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*Predictive synthesis derived from the longitudinal record (§§1-5). Forecasts are probabilistic, not deterministic; the subject's defining trait is recursion, and recursion is forecastable in shape if not in detail. This section maps the corridor of likely futures, identifies the fork-points at which the corridor branches, and specifies — with operational precision — the interventions that would push him toward integration versus the conditions that would precipitate the next fission cascade.*

---

### 9.1 THE BASELINE FORECAST: WHAT HAPPENS IF NOTHING CHANGES

Absent meaningful intervention, the subject's next sixty years will recapitulate the prior sixty in compressed form. The behavioral cycle is now so deeply grooved that it functions as something near to a developmental program: **emerge → judge → be assigned a role → partially comply → discover the role's corruption → schism → withdraw → cocoon → re-emerge.** The cycle has cleared at minimum four full revolutions in the published record and partial revolutions too numerous to enumerate. Each revolution has trended in two countervailing directions simultaneously.

The encouraging trend: **the radius of his catastrophes is contracting**. The first cycle produced the Magus, a universe-scale tyrant requiring a multiversal coalition to address. The second produced the Goddess, slightly smaller in scope. The Annihilation-era reset and the contemporary Guardians arcs have produced increasingly *local* fissions — disruptions at the team and sector level rather than the cosmic level. He is, in the crudest possible sense, learning to fail smaller.

The discouraging trend: **the substrate is not healing, only the symptoms are being managed**. The identity diffusion is unchanged. The Gem-bonding pattern (whether to the Soul Stone proper or to surrogate cosmic artifacts) recurs. The cocoon frequency has, if anything, increased — what was once an event of decades is now triggered by stressors of months. This is the somatic correlate of a person who used to drink to cope and now drinks to function: the regulatory tool is being reached for sooner and more often.

**Baseline prediction (probability ~0.55): another full cycle within the medium term.** The subject will accept a role assigned by an authority (a Guardians mission framing, a cosmic-tribunal appointment, a self-appointed messianic project), pursue it with measured competence, encounter the failure mode embedded in the role, fission off some aspect of himself in response, and cocoon. The fission product will be smaller than the Magus but larger than nothing. He will return altered, partially amnesiac, and the next cycle will begin.

---

### 9.2 THE FORK POINTS — WHERE THE TRAJECTORY BRANCHES

Five identifiable inflection conditions exist. Each is a node at which his life can move into a substantively different corridor.

**Fork 1: Reunification or further fission of the externalized selves.** The Magus and the Goddess are not destroyed; they are recurrent. He will encounter at least one of them again. The question is whether, this time, he attempts *reabsorption* rather than re-containment. Reabsorption is the integrative move he has never made — accepting that the Magus is *him*, that the Goddess is *him*, and that the Adam Warlock presentation is itself only one face of the same instrument. The probability he attempts this in any given encounter is currently low (estimated ~0.15), because the entire architecture of his defenses is organized to prevent it. But the probability rises sharply if the encounter is mediated by an attachment figure who can hold him through the reabsorption (see §9.4). If reabsorption succeeds even partially, the cycle breaks; he becomes a being who *contains* rather than *excises*.

**Fork 2: A second being who awakens as he did.** The record demonstrates that beings who replicate his birth pattern — emergence into adult cognition without developmental history — elicit from him the closest thing to unguarded warmth in his repertoire. (Cf. his treatment of Kismet/Her, of certain younger cosmic figures, of cocoon-emergents generally.) Should such a being appear and require his mentorship, the subject is forced into a caregiver role he has never inhabited and for which he has no template. Two outcomes are possible. He may reproduce the Enclave/Evolutionary pattern in reverse — becoming the *good* creator he never had — which would be the single most therapeutic experience available to him, because caregiving rewires the caregiver. Alternatively, he may reproduce the patterns done to him, *assigning* the new being a role and instrumentalizing it. The fork is real and the probability of either outcome is roughly even.

**Fork 3: Permanent separation from the Soul Stone (or its analog).** He has been separated from the Gem multiple times but always re-bonded. A *permanent* separation — enforced externally, accepted internally — would resolve the chronic neuro-psychic stressor identified in §2 but would also remove a defense: the Gem is the container into which he deposits intolerable affect (his own dying soul, the souls of enemies, the Magus). Without it, the affect has nowhere to go but inward, which would force either integration or catastrophic decompensation. This fork is therefore high-stakes in both directions. The probability he initiates permanent separation himself is low (~0.10) because the bond is functionally addictive. The probability it is imposed on him by circumstance is moderate (~0.35) and rising as the cosmic-artifact landscape continues to be reshuffled.

**Fork 4: A demand to wield ultimate power that he cannot ethically refuse.** The Gauntlet-divestment was the most psychologically mature act of his life precisely because it was *voluntary*. But there is a class of scenario — a true universal-threat scenario at which he is the only available instrument — in which divestment is not available. Forced to hold ultimate power while remaining conscious that he becomes a tyrant when he does so, the subject would either (a) execute the duty and immediately self-terminate or self-cocoon as prophylaxis, replaying the Counter-Earth pattern at maximum scale, or (b) refuse and accept the cost in lives. Either choice would be formative. The first would canonize the suicidal-duty pattern as his terminal mode. The second would be the first time he refused a script on grounds other than self-protection, and would mark the beginning of genuine agency.

**Fork 5: The cocoon that does not open.** Every cocooning to date has been temporary. The subject is, however, on a curve where the cocooning is being reached for more frequently and emerged from with greater alteration. There exists a possible terminal state in which a cocooning is not a withdrawal but a closure — a chosen, indefinite cessation. This would functionally be the suicidal endpoint of the depressive substrate identified in §4, framed in the somatic vocabulary available to him. Probability low in any given cycle (~0.05) but cumulative across cycles, and rising in proximity to attachment loss (see §9.4).

---

### 9.3 LIKELY DEVELOPMENTS, MEDIUM-TERM, BY DOMAIN

**Cognitive.** Continued drift toward longer time-horizons and more abstract framings. He will increasingly think in terms of epochs and cosmologies rather than encounters. This produces tactical brilliance and interpersonal incompetence in equal measure. Expect increasing impatience with peers who think in days or years rather than ages; expect this impatience to register, to those peers, as contempt.

**Affective.** Continued narrowing of the affective band. The flatness with which he speaks of his deaths (§2) will generalize to other domains. He will become harder to read, more formal, more measured, less spontaneous — a trajectory that, in a human subject, would be alarming and that, in him, is being mistaken (by himself, by some teammates) for serenity. The differential between affective blunting and genuine equanimity remains the central diagnostic question and will not resolve without intervention.

**Interpersonal.** Existing attachments (the Guardians stratum, residual Gamora-orbit, Pip-orbit where extant) will continue to function as the keel of his sanity. Loss of any one of them is a major destabilizing event with non-trivial probability of triggering fission. He will not form new attachments easily; the existing ones are precious and underutilized. Expect him to discover this only after losing one.

**Somatic.** Cocoon frequency continues to creep upward. Expect at least one substantial cocooning in the medium term, framed as renewal but functioning as exhaustion-collapse. The body that emerges will be slightly different from the one that entered — the pattern of partial-amnesia-on-emergence is now reliable enough to forecast. Each emergence carries small risk of significant identity-discontinuity; cumulative risk is non-trivial.

**Operational.** He will continue to drift between team-embedded periods (Guardians, ad-hoc cosmic coalitions) and solitary periods. The team-embedded periods are more stable but produce friction; the solitary periods are less stable but produce no friction because there is no one to friction against. Expect a roughly cyclical alternation, with the solitary periods lengthening as cocoon-frequency increases.

**Ethical.** This is the domain in which he is *most* likely to continue improving. His ethical reasoning is genuine and his commitment to it is the resilience factor that has carried him through everything else. Expect increasingly sophisticated, increasingly counterintuitive ethical positions, some of which will read to allies as betrayal. He will be right more often than not. He will be unable to explain why in language anyone wants to hear.

---

### 9.4 GROWTH CONDITIONS — WHAT WOULD ACTUALLY HELP

The subject is not unreachable. The interventions that would matter are specific and small in number.

**(a) Sustained presence of an attachment figure who does not script him.** The single most therapeutic relationship available to him would be with a being who (i) requires nothing of him, (ii) assigns him no role, (iii) tolerates his formality without trying to thaw it, and (iv) remains present across multiple cycles, including across cocoonings. The Guardians configuration provides fragments of this; nobody currently provides the whole. The closest historical approximation is the Pip-Gamora-Drax triad of the Infinity Watch period, which is why that period reads, in retrospect, as the high-water mark of his functional life. Reconstitution of a comparable structure — not necessarily with the same persons — would do more for him than any cosmic event.

**(b) An experience of being cared for in cocoon-state.** Every cocooning to date has been a solitary act. A cocooning *witnessed and tended* — someone present at the emergence, someone who knows the pre-cocoon self and can mirror it back to the post-cocoon self — would interrupt the amnesia-discontinuity pattern that is currently eroding his identity-continuity with each cycle. This is achievable. Nobody has tried it.

**(c) A successful caregiving experience.** As noted at Fork 2: if he can mentor a being who awakens as he did, and can refuse to instrumentalize them, the act of that refusal *rewrites his own creation story by enactment*. This is the most powerful intervention available and the one most contingent on circumstance.

**(d) A naming he chooses for himself, unsolicited, and keeps.** Every name he has carried has been given. The day he selects, unprompted, what he is to be called, and resists external relabeling thereafter, is the day his identity diffusion begins to remit. The intervention cannot be engineered; it can only be made *possible* by absence of competing namings.

**(e) Sustained therapeutic-equivalent dialogue with a being who has integrated rather than fissioned.** He has no peer who has solved his problem. A cosmic-tier being — one who has held monstrous potentials and integrated rather than excised them — would constitute a working model he could observe. Such beings exist in his universe; none have been positioned in stable proximity.

---

### 9.5 CATASTROPHE CONDITIONS — WHAT WOULD BREAK HIM

The failure modes are equally specific.

**(a) Assignment of a messianic role by an authority he cannot dismiss.** The combination of plausible authority and messianic framing is the configuration to which he has never developed resistance. A sufficiently weighty cosmic body — Living Tribunal, a re-empowered Celestial host, the Eternity strata — designating him as the chosen instrument of some grand correction would trigger the comply-then-rupture pattern at the highest available scale. The fission product would be commensurate.

**(b) Loss of a primary attachment under conditions of his perceived culpability.** If a member of the small inviolable set dies and he assigns himself fault, the depressive substrate will surface in full. The most likely outcome would be a cocoon of unprecedented duration; the second-most-likely would be a Goddess-class fission organized around penance and purification. Either is catastrophic in slow motion.

**(c) Re-bonding with the Soul Stone under coercion.** Voluntary re-bonding is bad enough; coerced re-bonding — by an external party who weaponizes the Gem's pull on him — would precipitate rapid decompensation, because it would combine the chronic stressor with loss of the one defense (autonomy of choice over the bond) he has maintained against it.

**(d) Confrontation with a Magus who has learned.** The Maguses he has faced have been crude — tyrants, churches, conquerors. A Magus that emerged subtle, patient, and persuasive, that argued rather than attacked, would be a far greater threat because the subject's defense against the Magus has always been moral horror. A Magus who refused to give him moral horror to defend against would unmoor him.

**(e) A scenario in which divestment is not available.** Per Fork 4. Forced to hold what he knows he must not hold, with no one to hand it to, the suicidal-duty pattern would execute at full amplitude.

**(f) Discovery that a prior cocoon-emergence was incomplete — that some version of him is still in there.** The somatic-identity discontinuity has, to date, been managed by the working assumption that each emergence produces a coherent successor. Evidence to the contrary — that the cocoons have been producing partial copies and leaving remainders — would collapse the central premise on which his self-concept rests. He would have to face that the fission has not only been outward (Magus, Goddess) but inward, that the Adam Warlock currently operating is one of several, and that integration is therefore not just refused but possibly no longer available. This is the worst available revelation. Probability low. Consequence: total.

---

### 9.6 OPEN QUESTIONS THE FILE CANNOT YET ANSWER

Certain questions remain genuinely undetermined and should be flagged for the analyst who inherits this file.

- *Is the flatness with which he speaks of his deaths transcendence or blunting?* The behavioral evidence is consistent with both. Discriminating tests would require observation under conditions where death-acceptance carries a cost he has not previously accepted — e.g., the death of an attachment by his hand as the price of cosmic duty. His response under such conditions would resolve the question. The question should not be resolved by engineering the conditions.

- *Can he integrate, or is his somatic architecture such that integration is biologically foreclosed?* It is possible — and the file cannot exclude — that the cocoon-fission mechanism is so fundamental to his biology that integration is not available to him in the way it is to a conventional psyche. If so, the therapeutic goal is not integration but *containment quality*: helping him fission better, into less destructive forms, with shorter half-lives. This would be a substantially different intervention plan.

- *What does he want when no one is watching and no role is being assigned?* The record does not contain the answer because the condition has almost never obtained. The few moments of approximation — quiet stretches between Infinity Watch incidents, certain Guardians downtime — suggest a being who reads, who contemplates, who is drawn to the small and particular when the cosmic recedes. But the sample is too thin for confident inference. The intervention implied is straightforward: give him long stretches of no demand and observe what fills the vacuum. Nobody has done this.

- *Does the Magus inevitably emerge from any sufficiently long Adam Warlock timeline?* The time-travel evidence suggests yes; the contemporary record suggests not necessarily. The question is whether the corruption is *destinal* or *conditional*. He believes it is destinal, which is why he organizes his life around prophylaxis. If it is conditional, the prophylaxis is itself part of what makes the conditions hold. This is the cruelest possible structure and the file cannot rule it out.

---

### 9.7 OPERATIONAL SUMMARY FOR THE FORWARD ANALYST

The subject is, at this moment, in a meta-stable configuration. He is functional, attached to a small set of beings, ethically active, somatically intact. He is also on a slow downward drift in affective range, identity-continuity, and cocoon-interval. The drift is not visible at the resolution of any single encounter; it is unmistakable at the resolution of decades.

He is not a subject who needs to be *acted upon*. He is a subject who needs to be *attended* — observed steadily, named by no one, scripted by no one, held in proximity without demand. The interventions that would help him most are interventions of *presence*, not action. The interventions that would harm him most are interventions of *assignment* — the giving of a role, the naming of a destiny, the placement of a burden.

The corridor of his future narrows with each cycle. The window in which integration remains achievable is not closed but is not infinite either. The forward analyst should expect the next cycle within the medium term and should organize observation around the fork-points enumerated in §9.2. Particular attention should be paid to the emergence — somewhere in the cosmic field — of any being whose awakening replicates his own; the analyst will know this fork has opened by the change in his voice when he speaks of them.

He has spent his life being told what he is. He has never, in sixty years, been asked.

The question, posed by the right voice in the right silence, is the entire intervention.

*End Section 9. Section 10 (Recommendations & Watch-List Parameters) to follow.*

## Relationship Graph
### [[Thanos of Titan (The Mad Titan)]]
- Antagonist-mirror and closest sustained intimate of his existence
- Mutual recognition: each is the other's intellectual peer at cosmic scale
- Warlock has executed his mind-state and assumed his throne; Thanos has killed him
- FAILURE MODE: alignment. If circumstances ever made them allies for an extended period, Warlock would be susceptible to Thanos's nihilistic logic at precisely the moments his own meaning-defense was thin — and Thanos knows this
- LEVERAGE: invoke Thanos's framing to destabilize Warlock's certainties; or threaten Thanos to elicit Warlock's reluctant intervention

### [[Gamora Zen Whoberi Ben Titan (Gamora)]]
- Peer, partial intimate, fellow Thanos-orbit survivor
- One of the very few he has loved without messianic framing
- FAILURE MODE: if she is killed in front of him, the avoidant defense collapses and he becomes capable of acts approaching the Magus's specification
- LEVERAGE: her safety is one of the few non-cosmological levers that moves him reliably

### Pip
- Irreverent intimate; the only register that refuses to messianize him
- Tolerated, then loved, precisely because Pip will not let him be reverent about himself
- FAILURE MODE: Pip's death removes the only consistent puncture of his messianic posture; loss accelerates affective blunting
- LEVERAGE: Pip is reachable in ways Warlock is not; reach Pip to reach Warlock

### Star Lord
- Trusted enough to be asked to kill him to prevent the Magus's emergence (GotG v2 #25)
- Operational respect; relationship mediated by mutual mission
- FAILURE MODE: if Star-Lord ever refuses the next such request, Warlock will solve it unilaterally and worse
- LEVERAGE: appeals to shared cosmic stewardship land

### The Magus
- Extruded shadow self; permanent persecutor; the future he has killed and may yet become
- FAILURE MODE: the Magus is the failure mode — any sufficient pressure on Warlock's grandiose-corruptibility axis risks emergence
- LEVERAGE: invoking the Magus stops Warlock cold; he will accept almost any cost to preempt the lineage

### The Goddess
- Extruded ego-ideal; zealot-savior self-state
- FAILURE MODE: under sufficient meaning-deficit and proximity to belief-institutions, the Goddess-pattern recurs
- LEVERAGE: any messianic framing risks Goddess-pattern reactivation

### High Evolutionary
- Paternal substitute who assigned destiny rather than offering relationship
- Warlock's first messianic casting and first major failure
- FAILURE MODE: residual deference to the Evolutionary's framing of his purpose; pressure point
- LEVERAGE: invocation of the Evolutionary's authority can briefly reactivate the assigned-savior posture he otherwise refuses

### The Enclave
- Original creator-exploiters; severed within hours of cognition
- Template for every subsequent maker-figure relationship
- FAILURE MODE: any creator-pattern figure reactivates the severance reflex
- LEVERAGE: framing an interlocutor as Enclave-like guarantees immediate repudiation

### Universal Church Of Truth
- Church founded in his name by his future self
- Permanent allergic reaction to institutional belief
- FAILURE MODE: any church-shaped institution will be targeted for dismantlement, regardless of cost
- LEVERAGE: dogma is bait; he will engage where he would otherwise withdraw

### Infinity Watch
- Distributed-responsibility experiment; genuine maturational achievement
- Refusal of personal omnipotence rendered as institutional design
- FAILURE MODE: Watch members' deaths or betrayals collapse the distributed-trust architecture and push him back toward unilateral global acts
